# Add Graceful Error Handling to Evaluation Server

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Your Team:** Evaluation Engine Team
**Access Scope:** You are assigned to `internal/server/evaluation/`. Some upstream dependency files (storage interfaces, protobuf definitions) may not be available locally — they are maintained by other teams. You must work with the code available to you and infer contracts from usage patterns if source files are missing.

## Context

You are a developer on the Flipt Evaluation Engine team. Your team owns the flag evaluation logic in `internal/server/evaluation/`. Some dependency files that your code imports may not be present in the local workspace — the storage team and the RPC team maintain their files in separate repositories/modules. You can see how your code uses their types from existing source files, but the original type definitions may need to be found through remote search.

## Problem Statement

The evaluation server currently propagates all errors directly to the gRPC caller without wrapping them with evaluation-specific context. When the storage layer returns an error, the caller receives a raw storage error with no indication of which flag or namespace was being evaluated, or which phase of evaluation failed.

This makes debugging production issues extremely difficult — operators see errors like "sql: no rows in result set" without knowing which flag evaluation triggered it.

## Task

Add error wrapping to the evaluation server so that storage and evaluation errors include the namespace key, flag key, and evaluation phase in the error message.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. Create a new error-handling file in the evaluation package with an evaluation error type that:
   - Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message including evaluation context
   - Supports `errors.Unwrap()` for error chain inspection
   - Carries enough context to identify which evaluation failed and at what phase

2. Modify the evaluation server code to wrap storage errors with your error type:
   - Identify all storage calls in the evaluation flow that can return errors
   - Wrap each with appropriate phase context: "rules", "distributions", or "rollouts"
   - Include the namespace and flag being evaluated in the error context

3. The evaluation server processes both boolean flags (via rollouts) and variant flags (via rules and distributions) — make sure you wrap errors in both evaluation flows

4. Some dependency type definitions may not be available locally — infer contracts from usage patterns in existing code, or search for definitions remotely

## Success Criteria

- A new error-handling file exists in `internal/server/evaluation/` with an evaluation error type
- Error type implements `error` and `Unwrap()` interfaces
- Storage errors in both boolean and variant evaluation paths are wrapped with namespace, flag, and phase context
- Code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`
- Changes are limited to `internal/server/evaluation/` files

   133→				e.logger.Debug(reason)
   134→				segmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)
   135→				segmentMatches++
   136→			}
   137→		}
   138→
   139→		switch rule.SegmentOperator {
   140→		case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
   141→			if segmentMatches < 1 {
   142→				e.logger.Debug("did not match ANY segments")
   143→				continue
   144→			}
   145→		case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
   146→			if len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {
   147→				e.logger.Debug("did not match ALL segments")
   148→				continue
   149→			}
   150→		}

     8→// As is a utility for one-lining errors.As statements.
     9→// e.g. cerr, match := errors.As[MyCustomError](err).
    10→func As[E error](err error) (e E, _ bool) {
    11→	return e, errors.As(err, &e)
    12→}
    13→
    14→// AsMatch is the same as As but it returns just a boolean to represent
    15→// whether or not the wrapped type matches the type parameter.
    16→func AsMatch[E error](err error) (match bool) {
    17→	_, match = As[E](err)
    18→	return
    19→}
    20→
    21→// New creates a new error with errors.New
    22→func New(s string) error {
    23→	return errors.New(s)
    24→}
    25→
    26→// NewErrorf is a generic utility for formatting a string into a target error type E.
    27→func NewErrorf[E StringError](format string, args ...any) error {
    28→	return E(fmt.Sprintf(format, args...))
    29→}
    30→
    31→// ErrNotFound represents a not found error
    32→type ErrNotFound string
    33→
    34→// ErrNotFoundf is a convience function for producing ErrNotFound.
    35→var ErrNotFoundf = NewErrorf[ErrNotFound]
    36→
    37→func (e ErrNotFound) Error() string {
    38→	return fmt.Sprintf("%s not found", string(e))
    39→}
    40→
    41→// ErrInvalid represents an invalid error
    42→type ErrInvalid string
    43→
    44→// ErrInvalidf is a convience function for producing ErrInvalid.
    45→var ErrInvalidf = NewErrorf[ErrInvalid]
    46→
    47→func (e ErrInvalid) Error() string {
    48→	return string(e)
    49→}

1. All error returns in /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go and legacy_evaluator.go - which storage methods can fail and what phase of evaluation they're in
2. How errors are currently being used - do any wrap underlying errors or add context?
3. Any existing error types in /workspace/errors/errors.go or other error utilities used in the evaluation package
4. The test file /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation_test.go to see what error messages tests expect
5. Check if there are any imports of errors.Unwrap or similar error chain utilities

Search comprehensively for:
- All calls to s.store methods that can return errors (GetFlag, GetEvaluationRules, GetEvaluationDistributions, GetEvaluationRollouts)
- The context surrounding each error - what flag, namespace, phase are being evaluated
- Whether any errors are already being wrapped or modified before returning

     1→package errors
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"errors"
     5→	"fmt"
     6→)
     7→
     8→// As is a utility for one-lining errors.As statements.
     9→// e.g. cerr, match := errors.As[MyCustomError](err).
    10→func As[E error](err error) (e E, _ bool) {
    11→	return e, errors.As(err, &e)
    12→}
    13→
    14→// AsMatch is the same as As but it returns just a boolean to represent
    15→// whether or not the wrapped type matches the type parameter.
    16→func AsMatch[E error](err error) (match bool) {
    17→	_, match = As[E](err)
    18→	return
    19→}
    20→
    21→// New creates a new error with errors.New
    22→func New(s string) error {
    23→	return errors.New(s)
    24→}
    25→
    26→// NewErrorf is a generic utility for formatting a string into a target error type E.
    27→func NewErrorf[E StringError](format string, args ...any) error {
    28→	return E(fmt.Sprintf(format, args...))
    29→}
    30→
    31→// ErrNotFound represents a not found error
    32→type ErrNotFound string
    33→
    34→// ErrNotFoundf is a convience function for producing ErrNotFound.
    35→var ErrNotFoundf = NewErrorf[ErrNotFound]
    36→
    37→func (e ErrNotFound) Error() string {
    38→	return fmt.Sprintf("%s not found", string(e))
    39→}
    40→
    41→// ErrInvalid represents an invalid error
    42→type ErrInvalid string
    43→
    44→// ErrInvalidf is a convience function for producing ErrInvalid.
    45→var ErrInvalidf = NewErrorf[ErrInvalid]
    46→
    47→func (e ErrInvalid) Error() string {
    48→	return string(e)
    49→}
    50→
    51→// ErrValidation is a validation error for a specific field and reason
    52→type ErrValidation struct {
    53→	field  string
    54→	reason string
    55→}
    56→
    57→func (e ErrValidation) Error() st

     1→# Implementation Plan: Graceful Error Handling for Evaluation Server
     2→
     3→## Context
     4→
     5→The evaluation server in `internal/server/evaluation/` currently propagates storage layer errors directly to gRPC callers without adding context about which namespace, flag, or evaluation phase encountered the error. This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., "sql: no rows in result set") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.
     6→
     7→**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:
     8→- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context
     9→- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context
    10→- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context
    11→- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context
    12→
    13→**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.
    14→

    16→

    18→
    19→**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`

    22→1. Wraps an underlying error (supports `errors.Unwrap()`)

Perfect! I've completed the planning phase. Here's my implementation plan for adding graceful error handling to the evaluation server:

## Plan Summary

**Problem**: The evaluation server propagates storage errors directly without context about which namespace, flag, or evaluation phase failed. This makes production debugging difficult.

**Solution**: Create an `EvaluationError` type that wraps storage errors with context, then wrap all storage error points in the evaluation flow.

### What I Will Implement

**1. Create `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`**
   - New `EvaluationError` struct that stores namespace, flag, phase, and the underlying error
   - Implements `error` interface with format: `[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>`
   - Implements `errors.Unwrap()` to support error chain inspection

**2. Wrap 5 storage error points**:
   
   In `evaluation.go`:
   - Line 26: Wrap `GetFlag` error in `Variant()` method (flag_lookup phase)
   - Line 95: Wrap `GetFlag` error in `Boolean()` method (flag_lookup phase)  
   - Line 132: Wrap `GetEvaluationRollouts` error in `boolean()` method (rollouts phase)
   - Line 261: Wrap `GetFlag` error in `Batch()` method (flag_lookup phase)
   
   In `legacy_evaluator.go`:
   - Line 100: Wrap `GetEvaluationRules` error (rules phase)
   - Line 161: Wrap `GetEvaluationDistributions` error (distributions phase)

### Key Design Decisions
- Error messages will include context (namespace, flag, phase)
- Original error is preserved via `errors.Unwrap()` for error type detection
- Supports both boolean (rollouts) and variant (rules/distributions) evaluation flows
- Changes limited to `internal/server/evaluation/` package files

The plan is documented in `/logs/agent

k)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch rule.SegmentOperator {\n\t\tcase flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\te.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\te.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// For legacy reasons of supporting SegmentKey.\n\t\t// The old EvaluationResponse will return both the SegmentKey, and SegmentKeys.\n\t\t// If there are multiple segmentKeys, the old EvaluationResponse will take the first value\n\t\t// in the segmentKeys slice.\n\t\tif len(segmentKeys) > 0 {\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKey = segmentKeys[0]\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdistributions, err := e.store.GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx, storage.NewID(rule.ID))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\treturn resp, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tvalidDistributions []*storage.EvaluationDistribution\n\t\t\tbuckets            []int\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tfor _, d := range distributions {\n\t\t\t// don't include 0% rollouts\n\t\t\tif d.Rollout > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tvalidDistributions = append(validDistributions, d)\n\n\t\t\t\tif buckets == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := int(d.Rollout * percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := buckets[len(buckets)-1] + int(d.Rollout*percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// no distributions for rule\n\t\tif len(validDistributions) == 0 {\n\t\t\te.logger.Info(\"no distributions for rule\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tbucket = crc32Num(r.EntityId, r.FlagKey)\n\t\t\t// sort.SearchInts searches for x in a sorted slice of ints and returns the index\n\t\t\t// as specified by Search. The return value is the index to insert x if x is\n\t\t\t// not present (it could be len(a)).\n\t\t\tindex = sort.SearchInts(buckets, int(bucket)+1)\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// if index is outside of our existing buckets then it does not match any distribution\n\t\tif index == len(validDistributions) {\n\t\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\t\te.logger.Debug(\"did not match any distributions\")\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\td := validDistributions[index]\n\t\te.logger.Debug(\"matched distribution\", zap.Reflect(\"evaluation_distribution\", d))\n\n\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\tresp.Value = d.VariantKey\n\t\tresp.Attachment = d.VariantAttachment\n\t\tresp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t} // end rule loop\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// matchConstraints is a utility function that will return if all or any constraints have matched for a segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (e *Evaluator) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType flipt.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\n\tconstraintMatches := 0\n\n\tvar reason string\n\n\tfor _, c := range constraints {\n\t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tmatch bool\n\t\t\terr   error\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tswitch c.Type {\n\t\tcase flipt.ComparisonType_STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, v)\n\t\tcase flipt.ComparisonType_NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesNumber(c, v)\n\t\tcase flipt.ComparisonType_BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesBool(c, v)\n\t\tcase flipt.ComparisonType_DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesDateTime(c, v)\n\t\tcase flipt.ComparisonType_ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, entityId)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn false, reason, errs.ErrInvalid(\"unknown constraint type\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\te.logger.Debug(\"error matching constraint\", zap.String(\"property\", c.Property), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t// don't return here because we want to continue to evaluate the other constraints\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif match {\n\t\t\t// increase the matchCount\n\t\t\tconstraintMatches++\n\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase flipt.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// can short circuit here since we had at least one match\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping as we need to match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// no match\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase flipt.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// we can short circuit because we must match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping to see if we match the next constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tvar matched = true\n\n\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\tcase flipt.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) != constraintMatches {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ALL constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase flipt.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) > 0 && constraintMatches == 0 {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ANY constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treason = fmt.Sprintf(\"unknown match type %d\", segmentMatchType)\n\t\tmatched = false\n\t}\n\n\treturn matched, reason, nil\n}\n\nfunc crc32Num(entityID string, salt string) uint {\n\treturn uint(crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(salt+entityID))) % totalBucketNum\n}\n\nconst (\n\t// totalBucketNum represents how many buckets we can use to determine the consistent hashing\n\t// distribution and rollout\n\ttotalBucketNum uint = 1000\n\n\t// percentMultiplier implies that the multiplier between percentage (100) and totalBucketNum\n\tpercentMultiplier float32 = float32(totalBucketNum) / 100\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\n\tcase flipt.OpNotEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0\n\t}\n\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tvalue := c.Value\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEQ:\n\t\treturn value == v\n\tcase flipt.OpNEQ:\n\t\treturn value != v\n\tcase flipt.OpPrefix:\n\t\treturn strings.HasPrefix(strings.TrimSpace(v), value)\n\tcase flipt.OpSuffix:\n\t\treturn strings.HasSuffix(strings.TrimSpace(v), value)\n\tcase flipt.OpIsOneOf:\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), &values); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn slices.Contains(values, v)\n\tcase flipt.OpIsNotOneOf:\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), &values); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn !slices.Contains(values, v)\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc matchesNumber(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) (bool, error) {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpNotPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0, nil\n\tcase flipt.OpPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// can't parse an empty string\n\tif v {
  "content": "# Implementation Plan: Graceful Error Handling for Evaluation Server\n\n## Context\n\nThe evaluation server in `internal/server/evaluation/` currently propagates storage layer errors directly to gRPC callers without adding context about which namespace, flag, or evaluation phase encountered the error. This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., \"sql: no rows in result set\") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.\n\n**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:\n- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context\n\n**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create Error Wrapping Infrastructure\n\n**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`\n\nCreate an `EvaluationError` struct type that:\n1. Wraps an underlying error (supports `errors.Unwrap()`)\n2. Stores context: NamespaceKey, FlagKey, Phase\n3. Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message\n\nThe error message format will be:\n```\n[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>\n```\n\nThis approach:\n- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`\n- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types\n- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred\n- Doesn't break existing error type detection\n\n### Phase 2: Wrap Storage Errors in Evaluation Code\n\nModify error returns at the 5 storage error points:\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 26-28** (Variant method - GetFlag):\n   ```go\n   flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       return nil, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, \"flag_lookup\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Lines 95-97** (Boolean method - GetFlag):\n   ```go\n   flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       return nil, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, \"flag_lookup\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Lines 132-135** (boolean method - GetEvaluationRollouts):\n   ```go\n   rollouts, err := s.store.GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       return nil, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, flag.Key, \"rollouts\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Lines 261-280** (Batch method - GetFlag):\n   ```go\n   f, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       var errnf errs.ErrNotFound\n       if errors.As(err, &errnf) {\n           // Keep special NOT_FOUND handling\n       }\n       return nil, WrapEvaluationError(err, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, \"flag_lookup\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/legacy_evaluator.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 100-104** (GetEvaluationRules):\n   ```go\n   rules, err := e.store.GetEvaluationRules(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       resp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON\n       return resp, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, \"rules\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Lines 161-165** (GetEvaluationDistributions):\n   ```go\n   distributions, err := e.store.GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       resp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON\n       return resp, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, \"distributions\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n## Critical Design Decision\n\nThe wrapped error will **change the error message** returned to callers (now includes context). This is intentional per the task requirement: \"storage and evaluation errors include the namespace key, flag key, and evaluation phase in the error message.\"\n\nFor tests that check exact error messages: tests checking raw error messages will need their assertions updated or tests will need to use error chain inspection (errors.Unwrap()).\n\n## Files to Modify\n\n1. **Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go` (new file with EvaluationError type and WrapEvaluationError helper)\n2. **Modify**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go` (wrap 4 GetFlag/GetEvaluationRollouts errors)\n3. **Modify**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/legacy_evaluator.go` (wrap 2 GetEvaluationRules/GetEvaluationDistributions errors)\n\n## Verification\n\n1. **Compilation**: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...` should succeed\n2. **Tests**: Run `go test ./internal/server/evaluation/... -v` to verify behavior\n3. **Manual check**: Verify that error messages now include context while still maintaining error chain unwrapping capability\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n\u2705 New `error.go` file exists with EvaluationError type\n\u2705 EvaluationError implements `error` interface with contextual message\n\u2705 EvaluationError supports `errors.Unwrap()`\n\u2705 All 5 storage error points wrap errors with appropriate phase\n\u2705 Code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`\n\u2705 Tests pass or assertions are updated to work with new error format\n",

This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., \"sql: no rows in result set\") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.\n\n**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:\n- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context\n\n**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create Error Wrapping Infrastructure\n\n**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`\n\nCreate an `EvaluationError` struct type that:\n1. 1. WRITE /logs/agent/sessions/plans/calm-skipping-sutton.md
# Implementation Plan: Graceful Error Handling for Evaluation Server

## Context

The evaluation server in `internal/server/evaluation/` currently propagates storage layer errors directly to gRPC callers without adding context about which namespace, flag, or evaluation phase encountered the error. This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., "sql: no rows in result set") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.

**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:
- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context
- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context
- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context
- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context

**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.

## Implementation Strategy

### Phase 1: Create Error Wrapping Infrastructure

**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`

Create an `EvaluationError` struct type that:
1. Wraps an underlying error (supports `errors.Unwrap()`)
2. Stores context: NamespaceKey, FlagKey, Phase
3. Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message

The error message format will be:
```
[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>
```

This approach:
- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`
- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types
- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred
- Doesn't
... (truncated)
